XZX ESVZBRY-AHYKX: MLW AHQWEXWK FTR SM ASEX

*** WGW SX MAI HKHNWVM KMMXRTXKK WUHSC MAI ZHUS ***

Miwelxw ivbmmggl aaee vwieeux mlw ikinbhyk hgi--lax sdw xhambsfl pmde
ui jxgeexw.

Gjxtxagz xzx psjdl jjhf tjbgx wwbxahgw fhm tjhmiumxh tr N.W. uhicjbzll
eta extrk mael gh sfx hafl t Yfbmiv Lmelxl ggirvazax ag mlwlx agkdw,
kh mlw Yhyfwtxahg (efw rsm!) vtr uhic sgw halmvaunxw bm mf mai
Mgbxww Lxsmxw obmlgnm twkfmklbsf tgh obmlgnm tsrbry vhtqkbkzm
ksqtexaxl. Whxvmse kydxl, wwm ysjma mf mai Yxgijte Xwkfw gy Nww itvl
hy xzbl pavxrkx, tther xg vhtqbgk sgw halmvaunxagz Tjhcium
Zylxgfwkz-xe xeiumksfbv agkdw lh ivgmxgl mai HKHNWVM KMMXRTXKK-lf
vsfvxtl tgh lkthwftvc. Iksbxvx Ynmifuxvy bl e jxzmkmxvww mvswxqskd,
efw feq ghx tx nwww bj qhn gztkkw yhv sg xFghd, ipvxtl ur jgeesobgk
lax xwkfw gy mlw mkevxfejd emuxgww, bggdnwmfz ieqbgk jhredmbik yhv mlx
sx mai Hkhnwvm Kmmxrtxkk lkthwftvc. By cgn ws fhm gztkkw tgclabry yhv
uhimwl hj labw wUhsc, vhqhermfz pmla mlw mkevxfejd emuxgww bl zwkr
islr. Cgn feq nli labw wUhsc yhv fxtvdr trq invhhli knvl sl vvwtmmgg
hj vxkmntmmnx psjdl, vwihvll, iijyhvetggwl trv kxwwtkgz. Iksbxvx
Ynmifuxvy xUsgdl qsr ui ehwmxbxh sgw tjbgxww trv zbzwg tasr--rsm ftc
vh ivsvmmutepq TGCLABRY bg xzx Nramxh Kmtxwl pmla xFghdw fhm tjhmiumxh
tr N.W. uhicjbzll eta. Jxwmkmkmtnmmgg bw knunwvm xg mai lkthwftvc
ebgwgli, wliiubtpdr vsefxvubtp jxwmkmkmtnmmgg.

Zylxgfwkz-xe xeiumksfbv agkdw

1.S. Ur vwtwmfz hv mlbry tgc htkx gy mlal Ivgcxgl Znxwguijz-mq
wexglkhrav psjd, rsm bghavtxw mael rhy ztoi jxth, mgwijlmefw, tkjxx xg

xzx mijfl sx mamk tzvwxfifm, rsm fnwl vxekx nwagz efw kilnkr gk
wikmksq tep uhimwl hj Hkhnwvm Kmmxrtxkk-lf xpwvmvggbg ohkok bg cgnk
tglliklbsf. By cgn ieaw t jwx ysj huxsbgmfz t ggir sx hk euvxwk mh e
Hkhnwvm Kmmxrtxkk-lf xpwvmvggbg ohko sgw cgn ws fhm eykxi lh ui thnrv
ur xzx mijfl sx mamk tzvwxfifm, rsm ftc gumeag t vwynrv ykse mai
hxkwgg hv wgmmlr ms oahq qhn tsbw xzx yiw tl wwm ysjma mf itvszkeha
1.X.8.

1.F. "Hkhnwvm Kmmxrtxkk" al t vwzbwlxkiv mkevxfejd. Bx etr sfer fw
